2.4.4 Formål med lenke (4 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Link text is not descriptive: 'Info'

<a class="decoration-none! border-b-none! !mt-12 color-body!" data-ec-id="pp:2.7002" data-ec-name="Info" data-ec-variant="N/A" href="https://www.nrk.no/informasjon/">Info</a>
Use descriptive text that indicates where the link goes (e.g., 'Read more about products' instead of 'Read more')
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MINOR

Link text is very long (125 characters)

<a class="decoration-none! border-b-none! !mt-12 color-core-blue-50!" data-ec-id="pp:2.7002" data-ec-name="Info" data-ec-variant="N/A" href="https://www.nrk.no/informasjon/">Info</a>
Use descriptive text that indicates where the link goes (e.g., 'Read more about products' instead of 'Read more')
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MINOR

Link text has redundant phrase: 'Gå til forsiden- NRK.no'

<a class="inline-block mb-[14px] min-w-[45px] min-h-[19px] text-white w-full" href="https://www.nrk.no"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="inline-block w-[74px] h-[26px] mx-auto" fill="currentColor" heigh
